data-social-tool="print">print</a></li></ul></video1><p>The <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/schedule">2020 NFL season</a> is just over a week away, so it's time for our annual ranking of the league's top 100 players. What can we expect from the game's best players?</p><p>We asked a panel of 46 ESPN NFL experts to rate players based on how good they will be in the 2020 season in comparison to their peers. Emphasis was entirely on expectations for the upcoming season -- that means <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29774920/source-los-angeles-chargers-s-derwin-james-injures-knee">injured safety Derwin James</a> won't make the list -- and predicting potential greatness, rather than past performance, career rsum or positional value. From those ratings, we were able to rank the best of the best, 1 to 100.</p><aside class="inline editorial float-r" data-behavior="article_related"><h1>Editor's Picks</h1><ul><li><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:1" href="/nfl/insider/story/_/id/29778368/2020-nfl-rank-snubs-overrated-players-surprises-experts-debate-our-top-100" class="img-link"><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/combiner/i?img=/photo/2020/0831/r738741_1296x1296_1-1.jpg&w=130&h=130&scale=crop&location=center"></a><h2><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:1" top 100</a></h2></li><li><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:2" href="/nfl/story/_/id/29429298/2020-nfl-position-position-rankings-50-plus-coaches-execs-players-make-their-picks" class="img-link"><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/combiner/i?img=/photo/2020/0519/r699870_2_1296x1296_1-1.jpg&w=130&h=130&scale=crop&location=center"></a><h2><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:2" href="/nfl/story/_/id/29429298/2020-nfl-position-position-rankings-50-plus-coaches-execs-players-make-their-picks" class="">2020 NFL position-by-position rankings</a></h2></li><li><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:3" href="/nfl/story/_/id/29234387/re-drafting-nfl-picked-128-foundational-players-all-32-teams" class="img-link"><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/combiner/i?img=/photo/2020/0607/nfl_redraft_cr_1x1.jpg&w=130&h=130&scale=crop&location=center"></a><h2><a name="&lpos=story:editorspicks:inline:3" href="/nfl/story/_/id/29234387/re-drafting-nfl-picked-128-foundational-players-all-32-teams" class="">We re-drafted the NFL from scratch: Mahomes in Cincy, Rodgers in Vegas, more</a></h2></li></ul><div class="button button-alt sm btn-related">2 Related</div></aside><p>For the second straight year, the <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/kc/kansas-city-chiefs">Kansas City Chiefs</a> and <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">New Orleans Saints</a> led the way with seven players apiece, and the <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/min/minnesota-vikings">Minnesota Vikings</a> joined them this year following the trade for pass-rusher <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3053044/yannick-ngakoue">Yannick Ngakoue</a>. Twenty-eight teams in all were represented by at least one player, with the <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/cin/cincinnati-bengals">Cincinnati Bengals</a>, <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/mia/miami-dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a>, <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/nyj/new-york-jets">New York Jets</a> and <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/wsh/washington">Washington Football Team</a> coming up empty. Positionally, edge rusher and wide receiver most populated the top 100 with 17 names each, followed by quarterback (15). And with regard to <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/26881107/2019-nflrank-predicting-nfl-best-100-players-season">last year's list</a>, 65 players returned for another appearance.</p><p>For each player, our NFL Nation reporters weighed in on his 2020 outlook and asked a player, coach or executive from the league what makes him so dominant. Then ESPN Stats & Information provided a signature stat, and fantasy analyst Mike Clay projected a stat line for this season. Here's the full list, starting with the reigning Super Bowl MVP:</p><p align="center"><strong>Jump to a notable outside the top 10:<br />
<a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#bosa">N. Bosa</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#rodgers">A. Rodgers</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#brady">T. Brady</a><br />
<a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#cook">D. Cook</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#ertz">Z. Ertz</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#chubb">N. Chubb</a><br />
<a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#sherman">R. Sherman</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#diggs">S. Diggs</a> | <a href="/nfl/story/_/id/29766900/nfl-rank-predicting-best-100-players-2020-nfl-season#kupp">C. Kupp</a></strong></p><p align="center"><strong>See more: <a href="/nfl/insider/story/_/id/29778368/2020-nfl-rank-snubs-overrated-players-surprises-experts-debate-our-top-100">Experts pick snubs, more</a></strong></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20170710_nfl_fpr/charts/_end_rule.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734794_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>1. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3139477/patrick-mahomes">Patrick Mahomes</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/kc/kansas-city-chiefs">Chiefs</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 2</b></p><p>Over the past two seasons, Mahomes was No. 1 in many key stat categories including QBR (79). And at 24 years old, he should only continue to get better. Plus, the Chiefs gave him yet another high-end offensive asset in the draft when they took running back <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4242214/clyde-edwards-helaire">Clyde Edwards-Helaire</a> in the first round. <em>-- Adam Teicher</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> He has played 36 games in his career, including the postseason, and never lost by more than one score or posted a Total QBR below 50 in a game. In other words, Mahomes has never had a below-average game. It's by far the most consecutive games with a QBR of 50 or greater to start a career since the metric was first calculated in 2006.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "If there was ever a player that was truly deserving of the largest contract in U.S. sports history, it's definitely Pat Mahomes." <em>-- Brett Veach, Chiefs GM</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 4,477 passing yards, 33 TDs, 10 INT (281 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734795_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>2. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16716/aaron-donald">Aaron Donald</a></h2><p><b>DT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/lar/los-angeles-rams">Rams</a><br />
Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 1</b></p><p>Donald declared, heading into his seventh NFL season at 29 years old, that he feels like he's in better shape than ever before. The two-time NFL Defensive Player of the Year led all interior linemen last season with a pass rush win rate of 24.5%, and that could still increase in 2020 if new defensive coordinator Brandon Staley's scheme goes as planned. Staley has made it his mission to get Donald, who absorbs among the most double-teams of any lineman in the NFL, into more one-on-one situations. <em>-- Lindsey Thiry</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Over the past three seasons, Donald has recorded the first pressure on 175 plays. The next-highest total by an interior lineman in that span is 99 (<a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14941/fletcher-cox">Fletcher Cox</a>). For context, the difference between Donald and Cox in that time frame is the same as the difference between Cox and the players tied for 53rd.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "It just shows up every day how hard he works in practice, how hard he works in the weight room, how hard he studies film. It truly makes everyone else bring their level up higher when they see the best player on the field, arguably the best player in this league, working as hard as he does every day. I expect him to have another Defensive Player of the Year type of year." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3046779/jared-goff">Jared Goff</a>, Rams quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 49 tackles, 10 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734796_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>3. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3916387/lamar-jackson">Lamar Jackson</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/bal/baltimore-ravens">Ravens</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Jackson became the second unanimous NFL MVP after leading the league with 36 touchdown passes and setting the single-season mark for rushing yards by a quarterback with 1,206. What's scary is he still can make strides as a passer, especially on downfield throws. Could Jackson follow <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3139477/patrick-mahomes">Patrick Mahomes</a>' path by capturing a Super Bowl a year after winning MVP? <em>-- Jamison Hensley</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Jackson posted a 91.0 Total QBR when facing man coverage last season, the highest in the four seasons in which that data has been tracked (NFL Next Gen Stats). His 25 touchdowns against such coverage were also the most by anyone with one or no interceptions in that same span.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's the best player I've ever been around, and he works hard. So, I think you are going to see an even more polished and an even more ready Lamar than you saw last year. That almost sounds unbelievable, but the guy is incredible, and he's a winner." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116365/mark-andrews">Mark Andrews</a>, Ravens tight end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 3,427 passing yards, 26 TDs, 10 INT (901 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734797_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>4. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14881/russell-wilson">Russell Wilson</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sea/seattle-seahawks">Seahawks</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: 9</b></p><p>Wilson led the NFL last year with 22 completions that traveled at least 25 yards beyond the line of scrimmage and has the most such completions of anyone since his rookie season in 2012 (139). The Seahawks have the speed at wide receiver to complement what might be their quarterback's biggest strength: throwing the deep ball. Seattle added Phillip Dorsett to a group that returns <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2577327/tyler-lockett">Tyler Lockett</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4047650/dk-metcalf">DK Metcalf</a> and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4212909/david-moore">David Moore</a> -- all of whom have 4.40 speed or better. Wilson's durability and his recent MVP-level trajectory, plus the potential for more explosive plays, set him up for a strong 2020 season. <em>-- Brady Henderson</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Last season, Wilson's 6.2 TD-INT ratio was the second highest of any player who was sacked at least 40 times in a single season (<a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/8439/aaron-rodgers">Aaron Rodgers</a>, 12.5 in 2018).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He works harder than anybody I know. From a mental standpoint, knowing the game, knowing offense, knowing defenses ... From a physical standpoint, the work that he does ... to make sure he's out there every week. It's second to none." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/11260/duane-brown">Duane Brown</a>, Seahawks offensive tackle</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 3,668 passing yards, 29 TDs, 9 INT (397 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734799_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>5. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2976316/michael-thomas">Michael Thomas</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">Saints</a><br />
Age: 27<br />
2019 rank: 10</b></p><p>Not only did Thomas shatter the NFL record with 149 catches last season, but he also shattered the argument that his success is tied to quarterback <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2580/drew-brees">Drew Brees</a>. When Brees missed five-plus games with a thumb injury, Thomas caught 50 passes for 616 yards and three touchdowns from backups <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16728/teddy-bridgewater">Teddy Bridgewater</a> and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2468609/taysom-hill">Taysom Hill</a>. <em>-- Mike Triplett</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Thomas has 470 career catches, which is 11 away from tying <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16790/jarvis-landry">Jarvis Landry</a> for the most in a player's first five seasons. But Thomas has that total through four seasons.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "His level of preparation, intensity, expectation level and just how he approaches each and every day and each and every game [stand out]. And there's always a place where Mike is gonna create some separation or give you a place where you can throw the ball where he can get it and the other guy can't." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2580/drew-brees">Drew Brees</a>, Saints quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 114 catches, 1,352 yards, 9 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734800_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>6. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3117251/christian-mccaffrey">Christian McCaffrey</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/car/carolina-panthers">Panthers</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 22</b></p><p>McCaffrey became the third player in NFL history to have 1,000 yards rushing and receiving in the same season in 2019. That's why the Panthers are building around him and why they gave him an extension that made him the highest-paid back ($16 million per year) in the league. Beyond talent, he has the work ethic new coach Matt Rhule wants the rest of his team to replicate. He's as complete a player as there is in the league. <em>-- David Newton</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> McCaffrey is the only player in NFL history with at least 2,500 rushing and receiving yards each over his first three NFL seasons.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I don't look at Christian as just a running back. We see him as a weapon. We see him as a person that can be a receiver, a running back, a returner. As important as anything else is, the true leader [he is] on the team, and he does everything the right way. I don't think he's the type of player you can pigeonhole into one position." <em>-- Matt Rhule, Panthers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 1,051 rushing yards, 735 receiving yards, 11 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734801_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>7. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14942/stephon-gilmore">Stephon Gilmore</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ne/new-england-patriots">Patriots</a><br />
Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 33</b></p><p>Gilmore became just the 12th NFL player since 2000 to post back-to-back seasons with at least 20 passes defended. Entering his ninth NFL season, the 6-foot-1, 202-pound Gilmore still has the combination of size, speed, athleticism and football sense that makes him a true lockdown corner. <em>-- Mike Reiss</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> As the nearest defender when lined up in press coverage against a tight-window target, Gilmore allowed an NFL passer rating of 0.0 last season with a league-best three interceptions, via NFL Next Gen Stats.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Everyone knows he's a quiet guy. We call him the Quiet Assassin. He doesn't want to let guys catch passes on him in walk-through and he takes that demeanor onto the field each and every day." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/12691/jason-mccourty">Jason McCourty</a>, Patriots cornerback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 56 tackles, 3 INT</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734802_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>8. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15795/deandre-hopkins">DeAndre Hopkins</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ari/arizona-cardinals">Cardinals</a><br />
Age: 28<br />
2019 rank: 5</b></p><p>Since he came into the league in 2013, there have arguably been only two other receivers better than Hopkins: <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13982/julio-jones">Julio Jones</a> and Antonio Brown. But while both are trending downward, Hopkins' stock is still rising. He's a 1,000-yard machine, hitting the number in five of his seven seasons, including 1,165 receiving yards last season and another 208 in two playoff games. His ability to play inside and outside makes him even more of a threat, and now he gets to take his talent to one of the budding offenses in the NFL. <em>-- Josh Weinfuss</em></p><aside class="inline float-r inline-track"><p><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/welcome?addata=ffl_drafttoday_inline" target="_blank"><img src="https://g.espncdn.com/lm-static/ffl/images/promo-cards/ffl-1320x528_02.jpg"></a></p><p><strong><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/welcome?addata=ffl_drafttoday_inline">Create or join a league today >></a></strong><br />
<strong><a href="https://www.espn.com/fantasy/football/story/_/id/26806852/fantasy-football-cheat-sheets-updated-2020-player-rankings-ppr-non-ppr-depth-charts-dynasty">Cheat Sheet Central >></a></strong><!--</p><p><a href="http://espn.com/fantasyfootball" target="_blank"><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/scribe/article_FFL_003.jpg" alt="" width="100%" class="imageLoaded"></a></p><p>More people play on ESPN than anywhere else. Join or create a league in the No. 1 Fantasy Football game! <a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/welcome">Sign up for free!</a></p><p>--></p>
</aside><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Hopkins and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2976316/michael-thomas">Michael Thomas</a> are the only players to post at least 100 catches and 1,100 receiving yards in each of the past two seasons.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's the total package ... you can move him in the slot and he can have that feel and savvy inside and then you can go outside and he can do his thing there. And that's one of the great appeals to his game when I'm watching him as a playcaller." <em>-- Kliff Kingsbury, Cardinals coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 93 catches, 1,144 yards, 8 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734803_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>9. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3040151/george-kittle">George Kittle</a></h2><p><b>TE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sf/san-francisco-49ers">49ers</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: 42</b></p><p>Kittle already has more receiving yards than any tight end through his first three seasons in league history, so what could possibly make him better in Year 4? Fresh legs and a deeper connection with quarterback <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16760/jimmy-garoppolo">Jimmy Garoppolo</a>, to name two. The addition of <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15860/jordan-reed">Jordan Reed</a> could help spell Kittle in addition to complementing him and creating more favorable matchups. Having a second full season with Garoppolo should also serve the duo well, meaning more big-play opportunities for Kittle. <em>-- Nick Wagoner</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Kittle caught 79% of his targets last season, the highest percentage in a single season by a tight end with at least 900 receiving yards since 2001.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I think we don't have to say how important George is to us and not only as being the best tight end to me in the league, but also the type of person he is." <em>-- Kyle Shanahan, 49ers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 80 catches, 998 yards, 6 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734805_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>10. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3122840/deshaun-watson">Deshaun Watson</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/hou/houston-texans">Texans</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 47</b></p><p>Watson lost <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15795/deandre-hopkins">DeAndre Hopkins</a>, but he has more depth at the position, including three speedy receivers in <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3052876/will-fuller-v">Will Fuller V</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16731/brandin-cooks">Brandin Cooks</a> and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16016/kenny-stills">Kenny Stills</a>. Watson has 47 completions of 30-plus yards since 2018, and that should be an area he excels in even more this season. <em>-- Sarah Barshop</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Watson joined Steve Young (1994, 1998) as the only players in NFL history to have 25 touchdown passes and five rushing touchdowns in multiple seasons. Watson is the only one to do it in consecutive years (2018-19).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "One of his greatest traits is that he really has an understanding and he can see the field really well. He makes good decisions. I think from where he was a rookie to where he is now, it has improved leaps and bounds and will continue to get better with all the reps and how well he really understands the pro game now." <em>-- Bill O'Brien, Texans coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 4,029 passing yards, 27 TDs, 12 INT (518 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734825_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>11. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116406/tyreek-hill">Tyreek Hill</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/kc/kansas-city-chiefs">Chiefs</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: 16</b></p><p>Hill's numbers were down last season mainly because he missed all or most of five games because of injuries. But he was still an effective deep threat. Nineteen percent of Hill's catches went for 20 yards or more, and his 44-yard reception in the fourth quarter of Super Bowl LIV sparked the Chiefs' comeback. <em>-- Adam Teicher</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Hill was considered open on 31.5% of his targets last season, the second-highest rate among wide receivers with at least 80 targets (<a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2576716/jamison-crowder">Jamison Crowder</a>, 32.8%).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He would have been a great center fielder. He has the unusual ability to follow the ball down the field." <em>-- Andy Reid, Chiefs coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 79 catches, 1,121 yards, 8 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734827_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>12. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3122132/myles-garrett">Myles Garrett</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/cle/cleveland-browns">Browns</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 21</b></p><p>Garrett has vowed to earn the offseason contract extension that made him the highest-paid non-QB in NFL history. There's compelling evidence to believe him. Over his first three seasons, Garrett ranked fourth in the league with 0.82 sacks per game. He has the talent and the experience, and now finally the help around him. <em>-- Jake Trotter</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Garrett beat his block by 2.0 seconds on 32 pass rushes last season, which was second behind only <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16716/aaron-donald">Aaron Donald</a> through Week 11 (NFL Next Gen Stats), when Garrett was suspended for the rest of the year.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Myles as a player, from the first day he has been on the practice field, you can tell he was something special. The way he moves and the way he bends, it's just stuff you only see in a few guys in the NFL. It's been really impressive. If he puts together a whole season this year, really there is no limit on his success." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16740/joel-bitonio">Joel Bitonio</a>, Browns guard</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 45 tackles, 11 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734828_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>13. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13982/julio-jones">Julio Jones</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/atl/atlanta-falcons">Falcons</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: 7</b></p><p>Jones continues to be one of the most explosive threats in the NFL and is arguably the league's top receiver. His career average of 96.2 receiving yards per game is the best mark in history. Jones' combination of size, speed and physicality makes him nearly impossible to handle one-on-one. The Falcons have to get him the ball more in the end zone. <em>-- Vaughn McClure</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Jones has six straight seasons with 1,300 receiving yards, tied with Torry Holt for the longest such streak in NFL history.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He is just so explosive. In and out of his cuts, he's shaking guys loose, creating separation. I've never seen anything like that.'' <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3924365/hayden-hurst">Hayden Hurst</a>, Falcons tight end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 89 catches, 1,246 yards, 7 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734829_2_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>14. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2580/drew-brees">Drew Brees</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">Saints</a><br />
Age: 41<br />
2019 rank: 11</b></p><p>No, the 41-year-old doesn't throw deep as well as he used to. But that makes his success even more impressive as he keeps adapting. Over the past two years, Brees had the two best passer ratings of his career and the two lowest interception rates of his career. <em>-- Mike Triplett</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Brees owns the top three single-season marks in completion percentage in NFL history, all of which have come in the past three seasons.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Every day he's coming to work with energy, like nobody's gonna outwork him. He's the hardest-working guy. He reminds me a lot of Peyton [Manning]." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13295/emmanuel-sanders">Emmanuel Sanders</a>, Saints wide receiver</em></p><p><a name="bosa"></a></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 4,010 passing yards, 30 TDs, 9 INT</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734830_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>15. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4040605/nick-bosa">Nick Bosa</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sf/san-francisco-49ers">49ers</a><br />
Age: 22<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Despite his rapid ascent to this spot on the list, Bosa is his own biggest critic. He spent the offseason self-scouting and came away believing he could have done more. That counts as harsh criticism considering Bosa was second in the NFL in total pressures (60) as a rookie. But Bosa says he wants to do a better job finishing his rushes and going into games with a better plan, both of which should allow him to improve on the 9.0 sacks he had as a rookie and solidify himself as one of the game's best young edge rushers. <em>-- Nick Wagoner</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Bosa's pass rush win rate was tops among rookies at 21.8%. Bosa was one of three rookies with a sack, forced fumble, fumble recovery and an interception in 2019 (<a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4035434/devin-white">Devin White</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4036261/devin-bush">Devin Bush</a>).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I think very highly of Nick and think he can do anything he wants to out there. He's extremely talented and he worked extremely hard out there so the sky is the limit for him." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2971275/arik-armstead">Arik Armstead</a>, 49ers defensive tackle</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 58 tackles, 11 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734831_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>16. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3929630/saquon-barkley">Saquon Barkley</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/nyg/new-york-giants">Giants</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: 12</b></p><p>There aren't many running backs who can top 1,000 yards rushing in a down year that was marred by injury. But Barkley is that talented. Now throw that talent into an offense that will put an even greater focus on the Giants' most dangerous skill position player, and it sets him up for a huge season in Jason Garrett's running back-friendly system. <em>-- Jordan Raanan</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Barkley had five rushes last season on which he reached 20-plus mph, second most in the NFL behind only <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116593/dalvin-cook">Dalvin Cook</a> (six).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "If he stays healthy, he's the best running back in the game. Most dynamic. He can score any time he touches the ball. He has proven that." <em>-- an anonymous NFC executive</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 1,162 rushing yards, 460 receiving yards, 11 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734832_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>17. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15847/travis-kelce">Travis Kelce</a></h2><p><b>TE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/kc/kansas-city-chiefs">Chiefs</a><br />

2019 rank: 18</b></p><p>The Chiefs do many things with Kelce, and his ability to do them well is one reason for Kelce's consistency. He lined up as a slot receiver or wideout most often, and he caught more passes (73) from these spots than when he lined up as a traditional tight end (24). <em>-- Adam Teicher</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Kelce is the first tight end in NFL history with four straight 1,000-yard receiving seasons, a streak that's still active heading into 2020.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "They're asking Kelce to do some things that are very, very difficult, and he pulls it off. It's maddening to not only our team but, I think, any team that plays the Chiefs." <em>-- Jon Gruden, Raiders coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 88 catches, 1,093 yards, 9 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734833_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>18. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3051389/joey-bosa">Joey Bosa</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/lac/los-angeles-chargers">Chargers</a><br />

2019 rank: 25</b></p><p>Moments before reporting to training camp, Bosa agreed to a five-year, $135 million extension that set a new defensive player record with $102 million guaranteed. The first Chargers player to earn a $100 million contract, Bosa produced 11.5 sacks last season, and he says he has a couple more moves in his arsenal that he's working to perfect as he enters his fifth NFL season. <em>-- Lindsey Thiry</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since coming into the league in 2016, Bosa has the fourth-highest sacks per game rate at 0.78. Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 61</b></p><p>Adams' 6.5 sacks last season were two more than any other NFL defensive back and 2.5 more than any other Seahawks defender. The Seahawks view Adams as a "chess piece," in the words of one source. They plan to take advantage of his versatility, including his skills as a blitzer, knowing they need to generate more pressure than they did in 2019. <em>-- Brady Henderson</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since coming into the league in 2017, Adams has 32 QB pressures (second most by a DB in the NFL) and the fourth-lowest completion percentage allowed (50.4%) as the nearest defender among safeties in coverage (NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "There's some real similarities [between Adams and Troy Polamalu] ... It's the nature that they play with is similar. Age: 27<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>He is coming off a season with career highs in passing yards (4,902) and touchdown passes (30) and is being paired with a coach, Mike McCarthy, who has succeeded with quarterbacks at every stop in his career as an assistant or head coach. With another 3,000-yard, 20-touchdown pass season, Prescott would join Peyton Manning and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14881/russell-wilson">Russell Wilson</a> as the only QBs with five straight such seasons to open a career. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since Prescott entered the NFL in 2016, he's tied for second in wins and game-winning drives, and tied for fourth in offensive touchdowns among starting QBs over that span.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Dak's so good at commanding a room, commanding a huddle, getting guys on the same page. Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 3</b></p><p>Mack had a mediocre 2019 (8.5 sacks, five forced fumbles) by his lofty standards. A former NFL Defensive Player of the Year, Mack remains a dominant pass-rusher with double-digit sacks in four of the past five seasons. Chicago believes the addition of veteran outside linebacker <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13984/robert-quinn">Robert Quinn</a> will make Mack even more dangerous in 2020. <em>-- Jeff Dickerson</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Mack is one of six players to have a pass rush win rate of at least 20% in each of the past three seasons as an edge rusher. The others: <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2577446/preston-smith">Preston Smith</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13976/von-miller">Von Miller</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13984/robert-quinn">Robert Quinn</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16802/demarcus-lawrence">DeMarcus Lawrence</a> and Jadeveon Clowney (NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><aside class="inline float-r inline-track"><h1>NFL on ESPN+</h1><img data-lazyload="true" data-src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2019/1126/original_20191014120652.jpg.jpg" class="round lazyload"><p>Relive the NFL's greatest games, original series and more. <b><a href="https://www.espn.com/watch/series/cb15d25b-8401-4254-b3b2-c55605d3101b" target="_blank">Watch on ESPN+</a></b></p>
</aside><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "You know, Mack's just Mack. He's going to always work hard and things like that, that's just him. That's his character and, you know, that doesn't change. He's working harder but he's always working hard." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3054847/eddie-jackson">Eddie Jackson</a>, Bears safety</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 51 tackles, 9 sacks, 5 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734847_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>22. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16737/mike-evans">Mike Evans</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/tb/tampa-bay-buccaneers">Buccaneers</a><br />
Age: 27<br />
2019 rank: 36</b></p><p>There were some questions about Tom Brady's underneath style of play meshing with Evans' above-the-rim style of play. But early on in camp, it's clear that not only can Brady hit Evans deep on passes traveling 35, 40 and 50 yards through the air, but Brady will help Evans open up a new dimension in his game: yards after the catch. Brady's ball placement has been strong, allowing Evans to make catches in stride. <em>-- Jenna Laine</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Evans has posted 1,000 receiving yards in each of his first six NFL seasons, joining Randy Moss as the only players to do that in NFL history.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's deceptively fast. He's obviously got the size, but his catch radius is ridiculous. The only guy recently that I can compare him to -- who was a little bit faster -- was Calvin Johnson as far as sizewise and a catch radius. But his numbers speak for themselves." <em>-- Bruce Arians, Buccaneers coach</em></p><p><a name="rodgers"></a></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 77 catches, 1,171 yards, 9 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734848_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>23. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/8439/aaron-rodgers">Aaron Rodgers</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/gb/green-bay-packers">Packers</a><br />

Immediately after the NFC title game loss, Rodgers pointed to how much of the offense the Packers never were able to install in Year 1. Plus, he now has the added motivation of showing everyone that Green Bay moved too soon to pick his heir apparent in the 2020 draft. <em>-- Rob Demovsky</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Rodgers has seen his Total QBR decrease in each of the past three seasons. His 50.4 QBR in 2020 was the lowest in his career.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I'll tell you what, he's been so much fun to be around not only on the field but in the meeting room as well. He's bringing great energy, he has been super positive and I'm really excited to be in Year 2 with him." <em>-- Matt LaFleur, Packers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 3,873 passing yards, 26 TDs, 9 INT (205 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734849_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>24. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3051392/ezekiel-elliott">Ezekiel Elliott</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/dal/dallas-cowboys">Cowboys</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 15</b></p><p>When he has played a full season, Elliott has rushed for at least 1,357 yards. Is he the same back he was as a rookie? He had just four carries of 20 yards or more in 2019, the fewest among the league's top 10 rushers. But the Cowboys firmly believe he is still a difference-maker and can become their closer under Mike McCarthy. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since entering the league in 2016, Elliott has a 55% rush success rate, highest in the NFL (how frequently a rusher gains 50% of necessary yardage on first down, 70% on second or 100% on third and fourth). During that span, he has also led the NFL in rushing yards (5,405) and recorded the second-most rushing touchdowns (40).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's a great football player, and at the end of the day, he's still had a very successful season and he's done a great job training. I know he spent a lot of time with Dak and that offensive group really getting himself in top shape. Age: 30<br />
2019 rank: 65</b></p><p>Jones has been perhaps the most underrated player in the NFL in quite some time despite being one of the league's most productive pass-rushers. He's coming off a 19-sack season (second in the NFL). His size and length make him a unique challenge for offensive linemen, and he has an aptitude for strip sacks if he can't get the quarterback down. Jones has a streak of five straight seasons with double-digit sacks, but the stat that's most telling about Jones is that he leads the NFL in sacks since 2013. <em>-- Josh Weinfuss</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Jones leads the league in sacks per game (1.02) since 2017. Last season, he generated a sack on 3.6% of his pass rushes, ranking him second in the NFL behind only <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16967/shaquil-barrett">Shaquil Barrett</a> per NFL Next Gen Stats (minimum 200 pass rushes).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Chan's a top-tier rusher. He's so different with his body type. He's so long, and it's kind of awkward, but he has power in that body, he has quickness in that body, and he obviously has length in that body." <em>-- Vance Joseph, Cardinals defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 49 tackles, 10 sacks, 6 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734851_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>26. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3042717/tre'davious-white">Tre'Davious White</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/buf/buffalo-bills">Bills</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 97</b></p><p>It's a massive jump up this list for White, who made a similarly sized jump with his play last season. The first pick of the Sean McDermott/Brandon Beane era cemented himself as one of the best cornerbacks in the league with an NFL-high six interceptions last season, including two in a playoff-sealing win against the Steelers in Week 15. White was a first-team All-Pro selection for the first time last year, and if he continues his level of play from 2019, that honor won't be his last. <em>-- Marcel Louis-Jacques</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> White had 84 targets without allowing a touchdown when he was targeted as the nearest defender in coverage. Only <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14942/stephon-gilmore">Stephon Gilmore</a> had more targets (96) without allowing a TD, per NFL Next Gen Stats.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "There's not a plateau in sight, and that's a good thing for us. I mean, he wants to get better, and as long as he's challenging himself and we're challenging him as well, he will get better." <em>-- Leslie Frazier, Bills defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 63 tackles, 3 INT</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734852_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>27. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14979/bobby-wagner">Bobby Wagner</a></h2><p><b>ILB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sea/seattle-seahawks">Seahawks</a><br />
Age: 30<br />
2019 rank: 20</b></p><p>You know you've set a high standard when you can have what some considered a down season and still be named first-team All-Pro for the fifth time in six years. Reasons to believe Wagner will get back in the conversation for Defensive Player of the Year in 2020: (1) He might not have as much on his plate as he did last season, when the Seahawks ran an abnormal amount of base defense; and (2) he'll have another playmaker in <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3115373/jamal-adams">Jamal Adams</a> for opposing offenses to worry about. <em>-- Brady Henderson</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Wagner has posted at least 100 tackles in each of his eight NFL seasons. The only players since 2001 with longer streaks are London Fletcher (13) and Keith Brooking (9).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "His consistency is really obvious. In everything that he does, he's just so first class, so on it, so squared away." <em>-- Pete Carroll, Seahawks coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 147 tackles, 2 sacks, 1 forced fumble, 1 INT</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734853_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>28. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3043078/derrick-henry">Derrick Henry</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ten/tennessee-titans">Titans</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Henry's jump comes after leading the NFL in rushing yards (1,540) and tying for the league lead in rushing touchdowns (16). The Titans will once again rely on Henry to be the focal point of the offense this season, especially after signing him to a four-year, $50 million deal. Henry's 6-foot-3, 247-pound build and his conditioning make him fully capable of another 300-plus-carry season. <em>-- Turron Davenport</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Over the past two seasons, no one has more rushing yards, rushing yards after contact and rushing TDs when facing a loaded box (eight-plus defenders) than Henry.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Derrick really does a great job when we go out on the field, he sets the tone. He works hard to take care of himself." <em>-- Tony Dews, Titans running backs coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 1,308 rushing yards, 212 receiving yards, 12 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734854_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>29. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3044859/chris-jones">Chris Jones</a></h2><p><b>DT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/kc/kansas-city-chiefs">Chiefs</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: 40</b></p><p>The Chiefs signed Jones to a long-term contract this year because he has unusual ability to rush the quarterback from a defensive tackle spot. Jones had a 20.4% win rate as an interior rusher the past two seasons, which is third best in the league, per NFL Next Gen Stats. He pressured Jimmy Garoppolo into throwing an interception in Super Bowl LIV. <em>-- Adam Teicher</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Over the past two seasons, Jones' 23.5 sacks when lined up at DT are second in the NFL, trailing only Aaron Donald's 30 such sacks.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Chris has really proven to be an elite player at his position and really one of the best defensive players in the National Football League. With his age and his talents, we're certainly expecting more great things to come." <em>-- Brett Veach, Chiefs GM</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 43 tackles, 7 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734855_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>30. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13971/cameron-jordan">Cameron Jordan</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">Saints</a><br />
Age: 31<br />

Watt</a></h2><p><b>OLB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/pit/pittsburgh-steelers">Steelers</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 83</b></p><p>As the cornerstone of the Steelers' defense, Watt has made big strides every year since he was drafted -- and 2020 will be no exception. Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>In a new rap song, teammate <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3124067/terrell-edmunds">Terrell Edmunds</a> calls Fitzpatrick a "cheat code." That about sums it up. The young, versatile safety barely scratched the surface of his abilities in his first season in Pittsburgh after joining the team via trade after Week 2. Fitzpatrick saw a ton of production early on with five interceptions in his first seven games before teams started avoiding him. This season, defensive coordinator Keith Butler plans to move Fitzpatrick around to keep him involved. Quarterbacks, beware. <em>-- Brooke Pryor</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> According to NFL Next Gen Stats, Fitzpatrick was targeted as a defender quite a bit less in the second half of the season. During Weeks 3-9, Fitzpatrick's target rate was 8.3%. He was targeted 16 times (2.7 times per game). In Weeks 10-17, Fitzpatrick's target rate was 3.5%. He was targeted eight times (exactly once per game).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "We tried to limit the amount that we put him with in the first couple weeks we had him and then we realized he could handle a lot more than we were giving him at times ... Obviously, we think he is a top-tier guy in the league." <em>-- Keith Butler, Steelers defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 68 tackles, 3 INT</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734887_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>43. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2980153/ronnie-stanley">Ronnie Stanley</a></h2><p><b>OT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/bal/baltimore-ravens">Ravens</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Stanley has developed into one of the most well-rounded blockers in the game. He excelled in protecting the blind side of NFL MVP <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3916387/lamar-jackson">Lamar Jackson</a>, allowing the fewest pressures (six) by an offensive tackle in 14 years. He also opened holes for the NFL's all-time best single-season rushing attack on the left side, where Baltimore averaged 7.2 yards per rush. <em>-- Jamison Hensley</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Stanley's pass block win rate (ability to sustain blocks for 2.5 seconds) has increased each of the past two seasons. His 94.1% rate last season as a tackle ranked fourth highest in the NFL, per ESPN blocking metrics powered by NFL Next Gen Stats.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I really think he took giant leaps last year as a player, as a professional. With Marshal [Yanda] gone now, Ronnie is really stepping up into that leadership position, and he does a great job just being himself and we love him. He's really becoming one of the best offensive tackles in football." <em>-- Greg Roman, Ravens offensive coordinator</em></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734889_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>44. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3129308/quenton-nelson">Quenton Nelson</a></h2><p><b>G | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ind/indianapolis-colts">Colts</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 52</b></p><p>The Colts have had a completely different offensive line since they selected Nelson with the No. 6 pick in the 2018 draft. His desire to play until he hears a whistle and be the ultimate teammate has trickled across the entire line. The Colts gave up the fewest sacks in the NFL in 2018 (18) and were No. 7 in the league in rushing with Nelson anchoring the line. <em>-- Mike Wells</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Nelson is the only drafted offensive lineman to be named first-team All-Pro in each of his first two seasons since the 1970 merger, per the Elias Sports Bureau. Nelson ranks ninth among qualifying guards since 2018 in ability to sustain blocks for 2.5 seconds, per NFL Next Gen Stats.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I mean, he is the best in the business. I mean, I think that is known across the league. He is the best in the game at the position, so to have the chance to learn from him is something that I'm really looking forward to." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3915470/danny-pinter">Danny Pinter</a>, Colts guard</em></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734890_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>45. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16709/zack-martin">Zack Martin</a></h2><p><b>G | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/dal/dallas-cowboys">Cowboys</a><br />
Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 39</b></p><p>Martin is as technically precise as any lineman the Cowboys have ever had. Teammates marvel at his balance and how he rarely goes to the ground. He rarely commits a penalty, too -- he has not committed more than two in a season dating back to 2015. Martin has the power to handle tough interior defenders but can also get out in space to lead <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3051392/ezekiel-elliott">Ezekiel Elliott</a>. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Martin's pass block win rate of 95.6% when lined up at guard ranked fifth among those players last season. Martin allowed first pressure on a play that ended in a sack one time in 405 pass-blocking plays all season (ESPN/NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "What I like about him is not only is he a great player but just his steady, professional approach. He brings such a high level of professionalism the way he operates. You can see that just during the offseason. He's one of those guys that's always in the building and does it the right way. He's a great example for our young guys." <em>-- Mike McCarthy, Cowboys coach</em></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734891_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>46. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13976/von-miller">Von Miller</a></h2><p><b>OLB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/den/denver-broncos">Broncos</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: 8</b></p><p>If Miller has his way, this ranking will look far too low by the time December rolls around. Miller was so frustrated with the 2019 season that he was already back working out just 72 hours after the season ended. He has flashed plenty of power and speed in the early going at training camp, and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14047/jurrell-casey">Jurrell Casey</a>'s arrival and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116733/bradley-chubb">Bradley Chubb</a>'s return from an ACL tear will also give the Broncos more options with Miller. <em>-- Jeff Legwold</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Miller's quarterback pressure percentage of 12% ranked No. 6 in the NFL last season, a jump from 26th in 2018 (minimum 200 pass-rushing snaps).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I do think he's had a hell of an offseason. ... I know he has worked extremely hard. I do sense that he's got a hunger to his game and to his attitude that I don't think he's had the last few years in the league." <em>-- Vic Fangio, Broncos coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 52 tackles, 10 sacks, 1 forced fumble</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r734892_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>47. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3917315/kyler-murray">Kyler Murray</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ari/arizona-cardinals">Cardinals</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>The reigning Offensive Rookie of the Year quickly established himself as one of the best quarterbacks in the NFL. Despite the Cardinals' 5-10-1 record last year, Murray shined, completing 64.4% of his passes, the highest rate among rookies, while throwing for 3,722 yards and 20 touchdowns against 12 interceptions. Murray got better as the season went on, figuring out when to take a sack and when to try to make a play. <em>-- Josh Weinfuss</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Murray joined <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13994/cam-newton">Cam Newton</a> as the only rookies in NFL history with 3,500 passing yards and 500 rushing yards.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "What stood out to me the most about Kyler is his progression. Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 23</b></p><p>Ertz has more catches through the first seven seasons of his career (525) than any other tight end in NFL history, set the single-season record for most catches by a tight end in 2018 (116) and has led his team in receptions and receiving yards in each of the past four seasons. Yet he still doesn't get the same respect offered to <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15847/travis-kelce">Travis Kelce</a> and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3040151/george-kittle">George Kittle</a>. Ertz was double- and triple-teamed for much of last season due to Philly's lack of weapons but should have a lot more room to work now that there are more playmakers on the outside to attract attention. <em>-- Tim McManus</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since 2016, Ertz's 3,719 receiving yards and 26 receiving touchdowns each rank second among tight ends in the NFL.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Ertz's track record is pretty impressive, what he's been able to do year after year. I love that guy to death. Age: 32<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Stafford was playing at a Pro Bowl level through the first eight games of last season, on pace for a 5,000-yard season after completing 187 of 291 passes for 2,499 yards, 19 touchdowns and five interceptions. A back injury forced him to injured reserve, but he returns in 2020 saying he's healthy. Darrell Bevell's offense, which allows Stafford to use his arm strength for downfield throws, and Stafford's better decision-making, honed from his years with Jim Caldwell, set the veteran QB up perfectly for a big year. <em>-- Michael Rothstein</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Stafford led all NFL quarterbacks last season with 10.8 air yards per pass attempt, and his 8.6 yards per attempt was second to <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14876/ryan-tannehill">Ryan Tannehill</a> (9.6).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "We see it all the time. Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 44</b></p><p>Sure, Leonard has been perhaps too consumed with outside opinion, drawing motivation from Madden ratings. But he's still an up-and-coming superstar. Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: 53</b></p><p>Lattimore is a huge reason the Saints have thrived since 2017, when he won the NFL's Defensive Rookie of the Year award. He routinely shadows opponents' top receivers.
