Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 59</b></p><p>At 25, Hunter became the youngest player in NFL history to reach 50 career sacks. He has strung together back-to-back seasons of 14.5 sacks (along with consecutive Pro Bowls) and is barely on the cusp of entering his prime. The elite pass-rusher made his way into the Defensive Player of the Year conversation in 2019, and this year he may finally get that recognition. <em>-- Courtney Cronin</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Hunter has forced 15 turnovers (interception or forced fumble) on QB pressures since 2016, the most by any player in the NFL.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "We've got a superstar in Minneapolis. Everyone talks about their edge rushers. This, that, Watt, Bosa. Yeah, well, we've got The Hunter." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2974353/ifeadi-odenigbo">Ifeadi Odenigbo</a>, Vikings defensive end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 70 tackles, 10 sacks, 3 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735122_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>56. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2976499/amari-cooper">Amari Cooper</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/dal/dallas-cowboys">Cowboys</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: 54</b></p><p>Cooper's route running is his best trait because of how he can create separation for Dak Prescott's throwing lanes. While he did not close last season strong, he was still a valuable third-down option, with 16 of his 17 receptions resulting in a first down. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Last season, Cooper was among the best outside the numbers, posting 50 receptions (fourth in the NFL), 761 receiving yards (second) and five receiving touchdowns (tied for seventh).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's such a smart route runner and I think he's got a plan in his head on every single route that he's running. So he knows how to attack leverage, he knows how to go after these corners and find the zones and different things. I think that's what makes him special." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14012/andy-dalton">Andy Dalton</a>, Cowboys quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 75 catches, 1,069 yards, 7 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735123_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>57. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116165/chris-godwin">Chris Godwin</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/tb/tampa-bay-buccaneers">Buccaneers</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>There were some questions about the pairing of Godwin and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2330/tom-brady">Tom Brady</a> because coach Bruce Arians prefers a big slot receiver to line up inside, rather than a quick guy, which is what Brady has had with <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/12649/julian-edelman">Julian Edelman</a> and Wes Welker. But Arians has made it clear that Godwin is a huge part of the offense, so it could be another 100-plus target season. Brady will appreciate his consistency, as it's rare Godwin has a drop. <em>-- Jenna Laine</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Godwin's 11.1 yards per target last season was the best among all players with at least 100 targets.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "[He is] a combination of Hines Ward and Larry Fitzgerald, and maybe a better outside receiver than both of them when I had them at the end of their careers. I knew he could do both, and that's going to equate to a lot of catches and a lot of targets." <em>-- Bruce Arians, Buccaneers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 88 catches, 1,190 yards, 8 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735125_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>58. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3043168/za'darius-smith">Za'Darius Smith</a></h2><p><b>OLB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/gb/green-bay-packers">Packers</a><br />
Age: 28<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>When was the last time a free-agent signing had this big of an impact on the Packers? Charles Woodson? Reggie White? Smith not only brought an energy and a vibe to the defense in 2019, he also produced in key situations. Perhaps best of all, he rarely left the field, playing nearly 1,000 snaps. <em>-- Rob Demovsky</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Smith's 14.8% pressure rate in 2019 was the highest in the NFL (minimum 300 pass rushes, per NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Z is a guy a lot of guys look up to just by the way he works on the field, off the field and prepares for opponents. ... When you start making plays and you're doing the right things, you don't have a lot of enemies, guys look up to you. At times, he'll be a talker, but a lot of it he does with his play on the field." <em>-- Mike Smith, Packers outside linebackers coach</em></p><p><a name="chubb"></a></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 55 tackles, 10 sacks, 1 forced fumble</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735126_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>59. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3128720/nick-chubb">Nick Chubb</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/cle/cleveland-browns">Browns</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Chubb was 47 yards away from winning the rushing title in 2019. Now, under new coach Kevin Stefanski, he'll be operating out of a multiple-tight-end, power-rushing attack that will revolve around him. Going into his third year, after which he'll be extension-eligible, Chubb seems primed for a monster season. <em>-- Jake Trotter</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Chubb led the NFL with 4.9 yards gained after close-in -- yards gained by a ball carrier after the first defender gets within 1 yard of him -- last season (minimum 100 carries, via NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "It's an argument that I always talk to my guys about and my friends. ... I honestly believe Nick Chubb is the best running back in the National Football League. I am going to continue to say that until I play somebody else and they show me otherwise." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4040983/mack-wilson">Mack Wilson</a>, Browns linebacker</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 1,269 rushing yards, 211 receiving yards, 11 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735134_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>60. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13978/tyron-smith">Tyron Smith</a></h2><p><b>OT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/dal/dallas-cowboys">Cowboys</a><br />
Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 50</b></p><p>Health is a concern because Smith has missed three games in each of the past four seasons, but he is still one of the best left tackles in the game. He gave up just one sack and two hurries last season. When Smith arrived as a first-round pick in 2011, he said his goal was to make the Hall of Fame. If he can continue to protect <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2577417/dak-prescott">Dak Prescott</a> as well as he has, he could very well end up in Canton. One more Pro Bowl appearance would be his eighth, the most in team history. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2577417/dak-prescott">Dak Prescott</a> has a 74 QBR when Smith is on the field, versus a 60 QBR when Smith is off the field.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "It doesn't matter how tired he is or what's going on or if it's ups and downs. He's going to be Tyron, and he's going to be 100 percent every play." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16802/demarcus-lawrence">DeMarcus Lawrence</a>, Cowboys defensive end</em></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735135_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>61. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15863/darius-slay">Darius Slay</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/phi/philadelphia-eagles">Eagles</a><br />
Age: 29<br />
2019 rank: 100</b></p><p>Since 2017, 36 defensive backs have seen at least 200 targets as the nearest defender in coverage. Only <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3126356/marlon-humphrey">Marlon Humphrey</a> and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14942/stephon-gilmore">Stephon Gilmore</a> (both 49.2%) have allowed a lower completion percentage than Slay (51.8%), per NFL Next Gen Stats. His efficiency dipped a bit last season, but he was often asked to play straight-up man against the opponent's best receiver. The Eagles' scheme should be easier on him, and he'll get a boost from being in a new environment following a rocky relationship with Detroit coach Matt Patricia. <em>-- Tim McManus</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Slay has put together six straight multi-interception seasons, tied with <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14974/janoris-jenkins">Janoris Jenkins</a> for the second-longest active streak in the NFL (Stephon Gilmore, 7).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He is super urging to get knowledge. He doesn't think that 'I'm done at becoming the best player I could possible be.' For a coach, that's always encouraging." <em>-- Marquand Manuel, Eagles defensive backs coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 53 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735136_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>62. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14945/harrison-smith">Harrison Smith</a></h2><p><b>S | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/min/minnesota-vikings">Vikings</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: 67</b></p><p>Coming off his fifth straight Pro Bowl, Smith remains one of the most complete safeties in the game. He covers, blitzes, calls the defense and is a major part of the Vikings' success against the run. Since 2017, Smith has allowed a 54.3% completion rate as the nearest defender (fourth in the NFL) and was second in ball-hawk rate (percentage of targets where the nearest defender made a play on the football) at 22.5%. <em>-- Courtney Cronin</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Smith was credited with 11 disrupted dropbacks last season (sacks plus interceptions plus batted/tipped/defended passes). The only safeties with more were <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15851/tyrann-mathieu">Tyrann Mathieu</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2969860/justin-simmons">Justin Simmons</a> and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3115373/jamal-adams">Jamal Adams</a>.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "We're always trying to think of more ways of how we can use Harrison because he is such a good playmaker. We probably should've used him, quite honestly, a little bit more last year." <em>-- Mike Zimmer, Vikings coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 94 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735137_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>63. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3042519/aaron-jones">Aaron Jones</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/gb/green-bay-packers">Packers</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Who knows what kinds of numbers Jones could have put up three years into his career had the Packers used him more earlier. But the important thing is that coach Matt LaFleur finally did, and Jones became as big of a focal point of the offense as the Aaron Rodgers-<a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16800/davante-adams">Davante Adams</a> combination. It might not be reasonable to expect Jones to repeat his 1,500-yard, 19-touchdown regular season of 2019, but it's hard to imagine him ever going back to being a part-time player again. <em>-- Rob Demovsky</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> According to NFL Next Gen Stats, Jones reached 15 mph on 53 carries last season. The only running back who got it in gear up to that level more often was Dalvin Cook (73).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "The biggest thing that I tried to expose him to is, 'Hey, here's some of the things that guys [like Todd Gurley and Devonta Freeman] that have played in this offense, some of the production that they've had. You can have the same type of production.'" <em>-- Ben Sirmans, Packers running backs coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 900 rushing yards, 368 receiving yards, 11 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735138_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>64. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3051890/laremy-tunsil">Laremy Tunsil</a></h2><p><b>OT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/hou/houston-texans">Texans</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Tunsil made his first Pro Bowl last season after being thrust into a new offense because he was traded nine days prior to the season. Tunsil said it was difficult adjusting to Deshaun Watson's cadence, but after one season together, he believes they are on the same page and "a lot of great things can happen." <em>-- Sarah Barshop</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Tunsil is as trustworthy as they come when taking on a pass-rusher one-on-one. He posted a 91.5% pass block win rate when he was not part of a double-team last season, which was the sixth-highest rate among NFL tackles. The average rate among qualifiers in this category was 83.7%.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Having a full [offseason] to know the whole package, to know the whole offense and see him work and see him get healthy -- it's been incredible. ... I know he's going to have another, even better season this year." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3122840/deshaun-watson">Deshaun Watson</a>, Texans quarterback</em></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735139_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>65. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16802/demarcus-lawrence">DeMarcus Lawrence</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/dal/dallas-cowboys">Cowboys</a><br />
Age: 28<br />
2019 rank: 30</b></p><p>Pass-rushers are defined by sacks, but even with just five sacks last season, after 24.5 in 2017 and '18, Lawrence was still a major factor for the Cowboys. He is a complete defensive end, in the words of former line coach Rod Marinelli, because of how he plays the run. With a more diverse scheme this year, Lawrence will operate on both sides and even come out of a two-point stance at times as the Cowboys mix their fronts. <em>-- Todd Archer</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Despite only five sacks, Lawrence posted a 25.8% pass rush win rate in 2019, good for fourth best in the NFL, per ESPN metrics from NFL Next Gen Stats. Lawrence is one of just three players to rank in the top 15 in pass rush win rate each of the past three seasons (Aaron Donald, Robert Quinn).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "To me, the work ethic and all that kind of stuff is there. ... DeMarcus, really, is just jumping in there and just, you know, pushing the envelope a little bit on different techniques, different things and seeing what's comfortable, what's not comfortable and things like that." <em>-- Jim Tomsula, Cowboys defensive line coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 56 tackles, 11 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735140_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>66. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3917676/ryan-ramczyk">Ryan Ramczyk</a></h2><p><b>OT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">Saints</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: 85</b></p><p>Having one of the NFL's premier right tackles is more important than ever in this era where elite edge rushers line up on both sides. Ramczyk shut out guys like <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16710/khalil-mack">Khalil Mack</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14927/chandler-jones">Chandler Jones</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13979/jj-watt">J.J. Watt</a>, Demarcus Lawrence and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16967/shaquil-barrett">Shaquil Barrett</a> last year, while getting the bump from second-team to first-team All-Pro. <em>-- Mike Triplett</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Ramczyk had just two pass block sacks attributed to him in 2019, tied for the fewest in the NFL among offensive tackles with at least 200 pass block plays.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's got a demeanor that never allows him to be flustered. He has a phenomenal knack of keeping a level head and being able to regain composure and recover off a move. And that's something you really don't see." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13971/cameron-jordan">Cameron Jordan</a>, Saints defensive end</em></p><p><a name="sherman"></a></p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735141_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>67. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14086/richard-sherman">Richard Sherman</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sf/san-francisco-49ers">49ers</a><br />
Age: 32<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Another year removed from the torn Achilles he suffered in 2017, Sherman returned closer to his previous All-Pro form in 2019, coming up with three interceptions and allowing a passer rating of 46.8 when targeted, third best in the league, according to Pro Football Focus. Now Sherman is back to full strength and playing out the final year of his contract. He has no problem finding slights both real and perceived to keep him motivated and should have no problem doing so again as the Niners look to him to lead the way for their secondary. <em>-- Nick Wagoner</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Sherman returned to his ball-hawking ways in 2019. He posted a 19% hawk rate, according to NFL Next Gen Stats, fifth highest among players with at least 250 coverage snaps at cornerback. That means he either had a pass defended or interception on 19% of his targets as nearest defender.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He has really taken that step from just being the wisest guy in the room but helping these guys learn and understand the pro game and how to be a pro and how to practice and approach that. You can't put a price on what he's meant to this defense." <em>-- Robert Saleh, 49ers defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 63 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735142_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>68. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3053044/yannick-ngakoue">Yannick Ngakoue</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/min/minnesota-vikings">Vikings</a><br />
Age: 25<br />
2019 rank: 68</b></p><p>Minnesota's defense regained its elite status when Ngakoue was traded to the Vikings. Early results from Ngakoue's first four years foreshadow a surge as he enters the very early part of his prime. Since the start of 2016, Ngakoue is one of just five players with at least 35 sacks and 10 forced fumbles in that span, according to ESPN Stats & Information. <em>-- Courtney Cronin</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Ngakoue has posted at least eight sacks in each of his first four seasons in the NFL. The only other players to do so since sacks became official in 1982 are Aaron Donald, Dwight Freeney, Terrell Suggs, Derrick Thomas, DeMarcus Ware and Reggie White.</p><aside class="inline float-r inline-track"><p><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/welcome?addata=ffl_signupforfree_inline" target="_blank"><img src="https://g.espncdn.com/lm-static/ffl/images/promo-cards/ffl-1320x528_01.jpg"></a></p><p><strong><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/welcome?addata=ffl_signupforfree_inline">Create or join a league today >></a></strong><br />

Like Bruce Lee said, 'I'd rather face a guy who practices 10,000 kicks once than a guy who practices one kick 10,000 times.' ... People know it's coming and they still can't stop it." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/11284/calais-campbell">Calais Campbell</a>, Ravens defensive end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 41 tackles, 10 sacks, 4 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735143_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>69. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15818/keenan-allen">Keenan Allen</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/lac/los-angeles-chargers">Chargers</a><br />
Age: 28<br />
2019 rank: 43</b></p><p>Allen has produced three consecutive seasons with more than 1,000 receiving yards, and he appears as motivated as ever to continue the trend. Over the offseason, Allen voiced his belief that he's the top receiver in the AFC West. With a new quarterback and newfound motivation to prove any doubters wrong, expect Allen to turn in another big season. <em>-- Lindsey Thiry</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Allen has caught 303 balls over the past three seasons; only Michael Thomas and <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15795/deandre-hopkins">DeAndre Hopkins</a> have caught more over that span. But Allen has generated more separation on his targets on average than either Thomas or Hopkins since 2017 (2.7 yards, according to NFL Next Gen Stats).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's a big receiver. He's not overly fast, but you can play him multiple positions. He's extremely intelligent, and you don't see too many guys that big that can go inside and get open the way Keenan can." <em>-- Anthony Lynn, Chargers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 83 catches, 980 yards, 5 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735149_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>70. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13980/patrick-peterson">Patrick Peterson</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ari/arizona-cardinals">Cardinals</a><br />
Age: 30<br />
2019 rank: 77</b></p><p>Peterson didn't make the Pro Bowl for the first time in his career last season only because he was ineligible. He missed the first six games due to a suspension for violating the NFL's performance-enhancing drug policy. But Peterson is still an elite corner and one of the best lockdown corners in the league because of his ability to play press-man coverage on an island. He intimidates quarterbacks from throwing in his direction and can take away half the field. <em>-- Josh Weinfuss</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Peterson didn't play in 16 games for the first time in his career in 2019, but when he's on the field, it's clear he still strikes fear in his opponents. Over the past three seasons, 73 players have played at least 500 coverage snaps at outside cornerback, according to NFL Next Gen Stats. None of them has been targeted as infrequently as Peterson (12.4% of his snaps).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I like where Pat's at. I like the focus. I like the drive. I like the look in his eye right now. He is so focused. He wants to be who we know he can be, and he wants the respect back, and I think he's on his way to earning that back." <em>-- Vance Joseph, Cardinals defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 66 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735150_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>71. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15797/lane-johnson">Lane Johnson</a></h2><p><b>OT | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/phi/philadelphia-eagles">Eagles</a><br />

Jarrett spent this offseason trying to elevate his game to yet another level, and 2020 promises big things. <em>-- Vaughn McClure</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since taking over as a full-time starter in 2016, his 189 tackles on rush plays trail only Damon Harrison Sr. (266), <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13281/linval-joseph">Linval Joseph</a> (214) and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2971282/deforest-buckner">DeForest Buckner</a> (200) among defensive linemen.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's a beast, man. He's a leader. He's a voice on the defense. It's always great to have him here. He's big-time." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3054962/keanu-neal">Keanu Neal</a>, Falcons safety</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 67 tackles, 7 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735176_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>87. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14958/demario-davis">Demario Davis</a></h2><p><b>ILB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/no/new-orleans-saints">Saints</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Davis, 31, admits he's getting better with age. But the first-time All-Pro is also getting overdue respect for how well-rounded he is. Davis has at least 110 tackles, four sacks and nine QB hits in each of the past three seasons. Only one other player has reached those totals even once in that span (Wesley Woodyard in 2017). <em>-- Mike Triplett</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since joining the Saints in 2018, Davis has registered 221 tackles and 25.0 disrupted dropbacks (sacks, interceptions, tipped/batted passes and passes defensed). Only two other linebackers have at least 200 tackles and 25.0 disrupted dropbacks in that span (<a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3056362/darius-leonard">Darius Leonard</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2978304/cory-littleton">Cory Littleton</a>).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "First of all, Demario is one of the smarter players I've played against and with. Sometimes in practice, he can tell what I'm running from just the smallest little split that I take. And he's athletic. Shoot, he runs better than some of the guys on offense, honestly." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3054850/alvin-kamara">Alvin Kamara</a>, Saints running back</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 113 tackles, 3 sacks, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735177_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>88. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4047365/josh-jacobs">Josh Jacobs</a></h2><p><b>RB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/lv/las-vegas-raiders">Raiders</a><br />
Age: 22<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>In rushing for a franchise rookie record of 1,150 yards, Jacobs set a high bar for himself. Then he went even higher, saying he wants to catch 60 passes in 2020. That's unlikely, though Las Vegas is betting on his continued ascent as a premier feature back. His preternatural field vision and deceptive power make it a winning wager. <em>-- Paul Gutierrez</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Jacobs averaged 2.25 yards after first contact per rush last season, ranking third behind the NFL's top two leading rushers (<a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3043078/derrick-henry">Derrick Henry</a> at 2.39, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3128720/nick-chubb">Nick Chubb</a> at 2.27).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He has got to stay wire-to-wire healthy, and we've got to get more out of him in the passing game, get him more on the field on third down. He had a great year last year, and we expect more from him this year." <em>-- Jon Gruden, Raiders coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 1,148 rushing yards, 280 receiving yards, 10 scrimmage TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735178_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>89. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3915535/denzel-ward">Denzel Ward</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/cle/cleveland-browns">Browns</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: 89</b></p><p>Ward was up and down in 2019 but was also battling a hamstring injury. A Pro Bowler as a rookie the year before, Ward still has the tools to be a lockdown corner. But after sitting out seven games through his first two seasons, he needs to show more durability as well. <em>-- Jake Trotter</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> According to NFL Next Gen Stats, Stephon Gilmore (minus-11.8%) and D.J. Hayden (minus-11.0%) led the NFL in catch rate allowed above expectation (minimum 300 coverage snaps). But just behind them sat <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3915535/denzel-ward">Denzel Ward</a> (minus-8.9%), who was actually targeted at the third-highest rate among those 70 cornerbacks (22.4% of coverage snaps).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I think Denzel has a chance to be a really, really good player. I like a lot of things about him physically, I like the person that he is, and [he] has great ball skills. We are excited about Denzel, and he realizes that there is work to be done." <em>-- Kevin Stefanski, Browns coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 61 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735234_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>90. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14876/ryan-tannehill">Ryan Tannehill</a></h2><p><b>QB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ten/tennessee-titans">Titans</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>After missing a total of 24 games from 2016 to 2018, Tannehill took full advantage when given the opportunity to lead the Titans. He joined Joe Montana (1989) and Sammy Baugh (1945) as the only three players to finish with at least a 70% completion rate (70.3%) and an average of 9 or more yards per completion (9.6). It's unlikely that he'll post those numbers again, but Tannehill is in a great position to show that last season wasn't an accident. His synergy with offensive coordinator Arthur Smith is peaking after being back together with the same weapons for another season. <em>-- Turron Davenport</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Tannehill became just the third quarterback since 1991 (when red zone data first became available) to finish the regular season with an overall and red zone completion percentage of over 70% (Steve Young in 1994, Drew Brees in 2018).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "It goes back to familiarity because everything was new to him last year. He's certainly further ahead. He was playing catch-up when he got here. I mean, he got hurt in the spring. He wasn't getting as many reps as the backup. So, not to speak for him, but just from what I've seen, there's certainly way more familiarity, and he's more ingrained into what we're doing." <em>-- Arthur Smith, Titans offensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 3,486 passing yards, 23 TDs, 11 INTs (205 rushing yards)</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735235_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>91. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3915239/josh-allen">Josh Allen</a></h2><p><b>OLB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/jax/jacksonville-jaguars">Jaguars</a><br />
Age: 24<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Allen set the Jaguars' rookie sack record (10.5) while only playing 60% of the defensive snaps. He'll be a full-time player this season, and in preparation for that, he showed up to camp noticeably leaner and said he spent the entire offseason working on his body and studying film. <em>-- Mike DiRocco</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Allen's 10.5 sacks are tied with <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3051389/joey-bosa">Joey Bosa</a> for the fourth most by a rookie over the past 10 seasons, trailing only <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13988/aldon-smith">Aldon Smith</a> (14.0), <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3116733/bradley-chubb">Bradley Chubb</a> (12.0) and Von Miller (11.5).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "You can tell physically that he put in the work in the offseason, which is a credit to him. And once we've been in the room, he has just a million questions. At times you're like, 'Hey, hold on, let somebody else ask a damn question.' But you know he's trying to take that next step, and that's the type of person he is, which is awesome for us as a coaching staff and as an organization." <em>-- Todd Wash, Jaguars defensive coordinator</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 47 tackles, 7 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735236_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>92. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2969860/justin-simmons">Justin Simmons</a></h2><p><b>S | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/den/denver-broncos">Broncos</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Simmons was a second-team All-Pro selection last season, and he's made it clear he wants even more moving forward. He can play down at the line of scrimmage in the run game if Vic Fangio needs him to, and he has the speed to play deep as well. Simmons has even been used at cornerback for a smattering of snaps in his time with the Broncos when the team has had injuries in the secondary. He's in a contract year, and if he plays like he did last season -- or better -- Simmons' price is only going up. <em>-- Jeff Legwold</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> According to NFL Next Gen Stats, Simmons had the second-lowest NFL passer rating allowed (34.7) when targeted as the nearest defender in coverage last season among those with at least 40 targets (<a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3121649/jc-jackson">J.C. Jackson</a>, 21.8).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "I have total confidence in Justin and him being able to go out and perform just as good or better than he performed last year. He's that type of player mentally and physically. [I'm] looking for him to do some great things this year." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13254/kareem-jackson">Kareem Jackson</a>, Broncos safety</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 89 tackles, 3 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735237_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>93. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2971275/arik-armstead">Arik Armstead</a></h2><p><b>DE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/sf/san-francisco-49ers">49ers</a><br />
Age: 26<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>In 2019, it was Armstead -- not <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4040605/nick-bosa">Nick Bosa</a>, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2971282/deforest-buckner">DeForest Buckner</a> or <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16707/dee-ford">Dee Ford</a> -- who led the 49ers in sacks (10.0), as he was finally able to stay healthy and put it all together. He was rewarded with a big contract extension in the offseason, and the Niners drafted <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4259491/javon-kinlaw">Javon Kinlaw</a> to replace Buckner in hopes the line will continue its dominance. But the biggest reason for optimism that Armstead should expand on his breakthrough season is Ford's return to health, which will allow Armstead to continue moving inside, where he's at his best as a pass-rusher on obvious throwing downs. <em>-- Nick Wagoner</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Armstead, <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13971/cameron-jordan">Cameron Jordan</a>, <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2976560/danielle-hunter">Danielle Hunter</a> and Joey Bosa were the only four defensive linemen to register at least 10.0 sacks and 50 tackles last season.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's a big problem, literally. He can rush inside, he can rush outside. He can play the run inside, he can play the run outside. He's just dangerous. He's great with his hands. He's powerful. He's fast. It's a joy to play with him." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/16707/dee-ford">Dee Ford</a>, 49ers defensive end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 55 tackles, 9 sacks, 2 forced fumbles</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0822/r735238_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>94. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3895429/jaire-alexander">Jaire Alexander</a></h2><p><b>CB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/gb/green-bay-packers">Packers</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Don't think Alexander is one of the elite corners? Consider that since he came into the NFL, only Stephon Gilmore (28) has more pass breakups than Alexander (24). And last year, he allowed the seventh-lowest completion percentage among defenders targeted at least 75 times, according to NFL Next Gen Stats. All but one player higher than him has made a Pro Bowl. <em>-- Rob Demovsky</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> According to NFL Next Gen Stats, among defensive backs with at least 800 coverage snaps over the past two seasons, only <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2513035/byron-jones">Byron Jones</a> and <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3052101/chidobe-awuzie">Chidobe Awuzie</a> force tight-window throws on targets more than Alexander (33.2% of targets).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Certainly, Jaire has established himself as one of the better corners in the National Football League, and he's just getting started in his career. He has so much in front of him." <em>-- Brian Gutekunst, Packers GM</em></p><p><a name="kupp"></a></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 64 tackles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735244_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>95. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2977187/cooper-kupp">Cooper Kupp</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/lar/los-angeles-rams">Rams</a><br />
Age: 27<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Kupp established himself as quarterback Jared Goff's go-to target during the first half of 2019, peaking with a seven-catch, 220-receiving-yard performance in Week 8. Expect the sure-handed Kupp to continue to expand his role and production this season as the offense adjusts to playing without running back <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2977644/todd-gurley-ii">Todd Gurley II</a> and receiver Brandin Cooks. <em>-- Lindsey Thiry</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Kupp played only 48% of his snaps in the slot last season, which was 37th among wide receivers (minimum 100 snaps). Yet his 783 receiving yards in the slot were the most by any receiver last season.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "Cooper is continuing to accelerate his level of play. ... He's been a really good asset for us, obviously, and I'm excited about his level this year as well." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3046779/jared-goff">Jared Goff</a>, Rams quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 80 catches, 997 yards, 6 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735245_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>96. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/2510863/eric-kendricks">Eric Kendricks</a></h2><p><b>ILB | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/min/minnesota-vikings">Vikings</a><br />
Age: 28<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Kendricks cemented himself as one of the league's top linebackers in a season where he had a career-high in run stops (35), pass deflections (12) and forced fumbles (2). He led the team in tackles for a fifth straight year and is a critical piece for the Vikings in maintaining a top-five run defense. <em>-- Courtney Cronin</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since 2016, Kendricks has recorded the sixth-most tackles in the league. And according to NFL Next Gen Stats, he has the second-lowest completion percentage as the nearest defender among all linebackers (minimum 150 targets).</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "That's a kid whose motor never stops. I think it doesn't stop at home. It doesn't stop on the field, in the meetings. It doesn't stop anywhere. That's how he makes all of his plays, because he doesn't stop." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15810/xavier-rhodes">Xavier Rhodes</a>, Colts cornerback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 116 tackles, 2 sacks, 2 forced fumbles, 2 INTs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735246_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>97. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/4047646/aj-brown">A.J. Brown</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/ten/tennessee-titans">Titans</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Few players maximized every opportunity to touch the ball like Brown did last season. Brown's 22.3 yards per catch were the second most, and he averaged a league-leading 8.9 yards after the catch. Tannehill quickly identified Brown as his favorite target, leading to Brown becoming the first Titans rookie receiver to post a 1,000-yard receiving season since Ernest Givens did so in 1986. Brown worked during the offseason with Tannehill, which should lead to more targets in 2020. <em>-- Turron Davenport</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Brown had five games with more than 100 receiving yards last season, which is the second most by a rookie in the Super Bowl era.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's a guy who is extremely talented. We saw that last year. Coming into Year 2, he's hungry, he's excited about the opportunity we have. ... He's running really well right now and I'm excited to see what he does this year." <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/14876/ryan-tannehill">Ryan Tannehill</a>, Titans quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 67 catches, 1,044 yards, 7 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735247_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>98. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/15683/justin-tucker">Justin Tucker</a></h2><p><b>K | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/bal/baltimore-ravens">Ravens</a><br />
Age: 30<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>With unprecedented accuracy and leg strength, Tucker is on the path to becoming the best kicker in NFL history. Over the past four seasons, he has missed only five field goal attempts when you exclude blocked kicks -- and only one (43 yards) has come from inside 50 yards. He has also recorded an NFL-record seven career games with multiple field goals over 50 yards. <em>-- Jamison Hensley</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Tucker is the most accurate kicker in NFL history, with a field goal percentage of 90.8%. He is the only player to score at least 140 points in each of the past four seasons.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's the GOAT. He has got that golden leg. I've got all the faith in him. I'm on the sideline praying. At the same time, I'm like, 'I know Tuck can do it.'" <em>-- <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3916387/lamar-jackson">Lamar Jackson</a>, Ravens quarterback</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 27 of 30 field goals, 43 of 44 extra points</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735248_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>99. <a href="https://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/13229/rob-gronkowski">Rob Gronkowski</a></h2><p><b>TE | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/tb/tampa-bay-buccaneers">Buccaneers</a><br />
Age: 31<br />
2019 rank: NR</b></p><p>Gronkowski might have sat out last year, but he looks light on his feet so far in training camp, and his connection with Tom Brady hasn't missed a beat. Whether it's a quick strike in the back of the end zone during a red zone period or Brady airing out a deep ball, the duo have hooked up for big gains a lot already in camp. The key will be keeping him healthy. <em>-- Jenna Laine</em></p><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Brady and Gronkowski have connected for 78 touchdowns, the fifth most by any quarterback-receiver combo in NFL history.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "He's huge. People were talking about how he has gotten smaller in the offseason. Then I met him, and he's so much bigger than I am. He's just a massive dude." <em>-- <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/17453/cameron-brate">Cameron Brate</a>, Buccaneers tight end</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 47 catches, 640 yards, 4 TDs</p><img src="https://a.espncdn.com/i/infographics/20160725_mlbrankfuture/greyline.png" width="100%"><img class="floatleft imageLoaded" height="250px" src="https://a.espncdn.com/photo/2020/0823/r735259_400x600_2-3.jpg"><h2>100. <a href="http://www.espn.com/nfl/player/_/id/3120348/juju-smith-schuster">JuJu Smith-Schuster</a></h2><p><b>WR | <a href="/nfl/team/_/name/pit/pittsburgh-steelers">Steelers</a><br />
Age: 23<br />
2019 rank: 35</b></p><p>Smith-Schuster's first season as the Steelers' No. 1 receiver was a disappointment in just about every way possible. He missed four games with injury, and without Ben Roethlisberger, he didn't come close to replicating the numbers he put up during his first two seasons in the league. He spent the offseason studying the offense and refining his body, and he comes into the 2020 season with all the motivation in the world: It's a contract season, and Roethlisberger is back. Smith-Schuster was a game-changing wide receiver as Antonio Brown's No. 2. This season, he has a stronger supporting cast around him that should make life a little easier as the top target. <em>-- Brooke Pryor</em></p><div class="ad-300"><div class="ad-center"><div class="ad-slot ad-slot-incontent2 ad-wrapper" data-slot-type="incontent2" data-slot-kvps="pos=incontent2" data-independent="true"></div></div></div><p><b>Signature stat:</b> Since 2017 according to NFL Next Gen Stats, Smith-Schuster has shined in tight windows (less than 1 yard of separation), as his 20.3 yards per reception in that area is fourth among wide receivers with 50-plus targets.</p><p><b>What they are saying:</b> "We all know JuJu is a playmaker. We all know that he is going to be a guy we get the ball to jumpstart our offense in a big way." <em>-- Ike Hilliard, Steelers wide receivers coach</em></p><p><b><a href="https://fantasy.espn.com/football/players/projections">2020 projection</a>:</b> 81 catches, 1,035 yards, 7 TD</p><p align="center"><em>Who was snubbed? See <a href="/nfl/insider/story/_/id/29778368/2020-nfl-rank-snubs-overrated-players-surprises-experts-debate-our-top-100">who our experts think were left off the list</a>.</em></p>
